     recipeList = null;\n+        randomList = null;\n+    }\n+    \n+    private static String getName(String token) {\n+        int i, j;\n+        char[] dest;\n+        String d;\n+\n+        i = char[initialStringLength];\n+        token.getChars(i, j, dest, 0);\n+\n+        d = new String(dest);\n+        String s = d.trim();\n+        s.replaceFirst(\"^0+(?!$)\", \"\");\n+        \n+        return(s);\n+    }\n+    \n+    private static String getValue(String token) {\n+        int i, j;\n+        char[] dest;\n+        String d;\n+\n+        i = token.lastIndexOf(\"value\");\n+        i }\n+    \n+    private static void simpleToken(String token) {\n+        if(token.contains(\"/imgdir\")) {\n+            status -= 1;\n+        }\n+        else if(token.contains(\"imgdir\")) {\n+            status += 1;\n+        }\n+    }\n+    \n+    private static void forwardCursor(int st) {\n+        String line = null;\n+\n+        try {\n+            while(status >= st && (line =  private static void translateToken(String token) {\n+        String d;\n+\n+        if(token.contains(\"/imgdir\")) {\n+            status -= 1;\n+            \n+            if(status == 2) { recipeList, randomList));\n+                resetMakerDataFields();\n+            } else if(status == 4) {    //close recipe/random item\n+                if(state == 0) \"reqSkillLevel\":\n+                        reqMakerLevel = Integer.valueOf(getValue(token));\n+                        break;\n+                                    \n+                    case \"tuc\":\n+                        tuc = Integer.valueOf(getValue(token));\n+                        break;\n+                                        \n+                    case \"catalyst\":\n+ case: '\" + d + \"'\");\n+                        state = 2;\n+                        break;\n+                }\n+            }\n+            else if(status == 5) {  // inside recipe/random item\n+                d = getName(token);\n+                if(d.equals(\"item\")) {\n+                    recipeItem = Integer.parseInt(getValue(token));\n+                } else {\n+                  }\n+                }\n+            }\n+        }\n+    }\n+    \n+    private static void WriteMakerTableFile() {\n+        printWriter.println(\" # SQL File autogenerated from the
